msg:Due to weather conditions in Guangzhou, the flight was delayed, so I decided to stay in Guangzhou for another night. So I found the New World Hotel not far from the airport on Ctrip. Let me talk about the good aspects first. 
1. When I arrived, the guy downstairs was very enthusiastic to help open the door and guide me to check in. 
2. Because I was with a child, the front desk staff took the initiative to provide children's toiletries. 
3. When I shuttled around the hotel, the service staff would take the initiative to greet me and ask about my needs, which made me feel comfortable and happy. 
4. The hard facilities in the guest room are good, and the entrance is divided into three parts, dry and wet. There is a small entrance hall designed for home, and a glass door is added in the sleeping area and the bathroom area. The hotel's sound insulation and privacy are very good. 
The bad aspects, 
1. There is no A4 paper in the guest room, and enough drinking water (the water is in a paper box), so you need to call the service center actively. 
2. Although the room lights have intelligent control, they are stupid and difficult to use. Many buttons conflict with each other, and the curtains are still manual at this price, which is very puzzling (all national brands under Huazhu can achieve automatic curtains). I accept it, but it can't be difficult to use, which reduces the comfort of staying.
3. The system actually rejected my late check-out permission on Ctrip. Fortunately, I took the initiative to call the service center and solved the problem.
I hope that the hotel management can optimize the small details in the future, and I wish it will get better and better.

msg:Let me give you the conclusion first. This is a hotel that really surprised me and made me fall in love with it. It is the best hotel I have stayed in in 2024.

[Hardware]
Because it may be a new hotel, the hardware is very good. The New World Hotel is under the Rosewood Group, so the decoration style and some toiletries are similar to the style of Rosewood. I will give you a few examples of how good the hardware is. The water in the room is not bottled water, but natural mineral water in a very high-quality paper box. The hair dryer is from Lefen, with a market price of about 600 yuan. It feels similar to Dyson. The yoga mat in the gym is from Lululemon, and the price is also around 600 yuan.

„ÄêService„Äë
This is consistent with most of the comments on Ctrip. It is very good and meticulous. First of all, when you arrive at the hotel entrance, there are staff to help you take your suitcase to the elevator entrance. Because check-in is done on the 9th floor, after that, the front desk staff will take you to the elevator entrance to the guest room. When eating breakfast, from entering the restaurant to sitting down, there are service staff at every distance within sight, such as helping you with tableware, pouring coffee, etc. The response speed is very fast. One thing I hope to improve is that the speed of collecting meals is too fast. I haven't finished eating yet, and when I went to get something, it was collected. The most impressive thing is that no matter where you are, the hotel staff will smile when they look at you or meet you. Smile can bring people closer, in any corner of the world.

„ÄêFood and surrounding environment„Äë
This is an aspect that I care about when choosing a hotel. I really like breakfast. All the ingredients can only be described in three words: just right. Take the food I ate as an example, seafood porridge, the porridge was cooked just right, with fried dough sticks, the fried dough sticks were not oily or dry, the egg rolls were just right in size, style, and saltiness, the orange juice was not too sweet (most orange juices are very sweet), the fried noodles and bacon were not too oily, and the bread was freshly baked, basically comparable to the bakery. The most unexpected thing is that you can order freshly made banana muffins, which are both beautiful and delicious. The interior environment of the restaurant is warm and cozy, and the exterior is a floor-to-ceiling window with a good view.

The hotel is surrounded by mountains and has good green plants, so when you are in the room, gym, and restaurant, the visual range is green, which makes people feel relaxed and happy

The above is my feeling, I will definitely stay here a second time.

Location: A little out of the way, but the surrounding area is very popular and very popular. There is actually a market on the street next to it, with stalls set up on the roadside. I like it very much.
Hardware: The hotel's hardware, decoration, and design have surpassed most hotels of the same level. As a sub-brand of Rosewood, New World not only has many shadows of Rosewood, but also retains some of Rosewood's control over quality and a**osphere.
The bedding in the room feels a little higher than the average five-star hotel. There is no bathtub, but the glass door is very good and the sound insulation is high-end. The furniture in the room is modern and simple, and the colors, patterns and designs are more homely, warm and comfortable. , relaxing, small and slightly exquisite, all the displays and containers can be seen to have been carefully selected. The wardrobe and under the sink are all hollowed out, giving a better sense of space. Personally, I like this new style of design.
A**osphere: Green plants and flowers are used very well. There are many large green plants in the light-toned environment of the public area, and flowers are also placed in many places, which are just right.
The lighting is also good. There are many floor lamps, wall lamps, and chandeliers, which create the overall a**osphere. The only thing I think is that the lighting is too bright. It would be more advanced if it was darker (personally).
Music, I didn‚Äôt pay much attention to the music when I arrived on the first floor, the lobby on the 9th floor, the lobby bar, the guest room aisle, and the elevator. However, when I had breakfast in the morning, the music in the restaurant was very good, and it was very suitable for the restaurant environment, giving a relaxed and cozy feeling.
Service: When arriving and leaving, the young man on the first floor was polite and proactive. The person who checked in should be Director Li. Bieber's service was good. When the elevator encountered a glitch when I arrived, he immediately comforted me and told me that the hotel was checking in. They repaired it and arranged a room with a better location for me. They were very sincere and professional. They called me one hour after checking in to ask about the room situation and if there was any need for assistance. They also asked about the check-in situation when they left. Restaurant: Western restaurant, breakfast is good and rich, much higher than ordinary five-star quality, especially the quality of food. The furnishings of the restaurant are very comfortable, the decoration and green plants are just right, with magnificent shadows (commendation), service staff and chefs, It's ok, it would be better to be more proactive and enthusiastic (don't imitate Huali's aloofness for this), the warm service is easy to perceive, just like Bieber at the front desk, sincerity is just right. The tableware, containers, and items in the western restaurant can be seen to be carefully selected.
I visited the lobby bar. The environment is very comfortable, the bar is exquisite, and the little sister is more enthusiastic. I haven‚Äôt tried the products yet, so I‚Äôll try it next time.
I only visited the Chinese restaurant. It was very good and a shadow of the beauty, but more compact. The person who led me should be the manager, a man who was very proactive, enthusiastic and professional.
The guy at the fitness center was very proactive and enthusiastic in his service. Although he was a little green, he was very professional and I was impressed by his dedication. He introduced almost all the facilities to me, and he was patient and attentive.
The self-service check-in machine at the front desk (although I have never used it), paperless check-in, and robot delivery are all respected and recognized by the younger generation. As a new hotel, they have done a good job.
This stay at Guangzhou New World Hotel completely changed my perception of the New World Hotel brand, and even made me look at it with admiration. Overall, it is really good!
